--Result--

--Query--

--Query--
SELECT dt3.f1 FROM t1 JOIN (SELECT f1               FROM (SELECT dt1.f1                     FROM t1                          LEFT JOIN (SELECT 1 AS f1                                     FROM t2) AS dt1                          ON TRUE) AS dt2               GROUP BY f1) AS dt3 WHERE dt3.f1 IS NOT NULL
